	$('.bottom-link').on('click', 'li a', function() {
		var t = $(this);
		var value = t.attr('title') ? t.attr('title') : t.text();
		gaEvent('ga-burger', __cosite, 'static_'  + value);
	});

	$('body').on('click', '.ga-burger, .ga-menu', function(e) {
		var t = $(this), l;
		var c = 'menu_burger';
		if (t.attr('class').indexOf('ga-menu') >= 0) c = 'menu';
		if (t.text() != '') { l = t.text(); } else if (t.attr('title') != '') { l = t.attr('title'); } else { l = '-no-'; }
		gaEvent(c, __cosite, l);
	});
